      <p> The Fists Of Justice militia are plotting to eliminate all cultists. </p>  <p> The militias usual gathering venue is <a href="/sandbox/nTR8nJOW/location/5A743Kp5"><strong>"The Wight & The Cursed Queen Tavern"</strong></a> in <strong>Ragthorn Meadows</strong> </p> 
      <p> The militia leader is a <strong>Gauzo Cunigunde</strong>, a level 8 Human Fighter.
